name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:One-Bedroom Suite
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Couples
info:6 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted October 30, 2021
msg:The staff were great. We made a number of requests including a couple of extra sewing kits for repairing an item of clothing that was torn, and they did everything that they could to accommodate us. A nice gym and swimming pool, table tennis room as well as a full sized snooker table in another leisure room, means that that if you're looking for something to do then there are definitely options. It was also nice having access to the outside terrace roof as well. My partner's favourite place though was without doubt the relaxation room which contained 6 massage chairs, just the thing to relax after a long day. If there was one small quibble it would be regarding the TV channels on offer which were slightly limited, but with other things to see and do it's only really noticeable in the morning when you might want to see a selection of news channels or likewise at night time. On a personal level, we did also experience a bit of a problem when we checked out. Upon arrival you have to pay a deposit of 1000yuan, which is fine. Upon checking out we were presented with our room service bill and I was asked if we wanted to have this taken out of our deposit, which we agreed was the easiest option. The room service came to a little over 900 yuan, and when they processed this I assumed the change from the deductions taken from the deposit would be returned to our alipay. When this didn't happen, we again assumed that it might just take time to show up on our account. But after checking out of our next hotel in Chongqing where we did the same thing, the change due was deposited straightaway into our account and that's when we realised that we had not been reimbursed by the intercontinental. We emailed them regarding this asking for our change and we've heard nothing back from them. So I would advise people to make sure they get their invoice at the end off their stay and to also ensure you get any change that you're due straightaway.

msg:The location, sanitation, environment and service are all very good, but the facilities are just so-so. Although the suite has many facilities that other hotels don't offer, for someone like me who has to measure weight every day, the scale is the most critical part. However, the scale in this room was broken. I called for repairs and it was still broken after the second repair. It was not easy to use until it was repaired a second time. As for the elevator, I always didn't know which elevator would open first after pressing the button. I had to stay focused all the time and see which of the six elevators would open, otherwise you would easily miss the elevator. In addition, you need to swipe your room card to enter the elevator. In a hotel of this level, the room card will not automatically display the automatic processing by floor. When carrying large bags and small bags, sometimes you have to swipe the card first, and then manually press the floor, which is very inconvenient.

posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:I stayed here many years ago, but now it has changed its name. The entrance to the hotel's underground parking lot is right next to the lobby on the first floor. The attendant at the gate is not very enthusiastic. When I arrived on the first day, I parked my car at the door and honked to wave before he came over. It may be because it is an apar**ent-type hotel. The underground parking lot is relatively large and clean. When you go out, you can park for free by telling the hotel the license plate. When checking in, a male attendant named Shi was at the front desk of the hotel. Because there were five adults staying, an extra breakfast was given, which I was very grateful for. The room has three bedrooms, one living room and three bathrooms (one bathroom has a bathtub in the suite, two are outside, and one bathroom outside the suite cannot be showered). There is an open kitchen with a dining table, a refrigerator, a washing machine and a dryer. One bedroom has a terrace. The room is arranged on the 37th floor, which is relatively quiet. The room has windows that can be opened, and electric curtains in the bedroom. There are many people during the peak breakfast period, not too many varieties, and the taste is okay. For takeout, you can inform the deliveryman in advance to let the delivery robot deliver it directly to the room. There are many places to eat around. There are several good barbecues across the street, and there are also several hot pot restaurants, which taste okay. There is also a famous palace pastry in Chengdu nearby.
